<h1>Tracker</h1>
<p>Ransomware Tracker to distinguishes between the following <em>threats</em>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Ransomware botnet Command &amp; Control servers (C&amp;Cs)</li>
<li>Ransomware Payment Sites</li>
<li>Ransomware Distribution Sites</li>
</ul>
<p>Each entry in Ransomware Tracker is tagged to a <em>threat</em> and a <em>malware</em>. Currently, the following Ransomware families are tracked:</p>
<ul>
<li>TeslaCrypt</li>
<li>CryptoWall (if you do want to know more about CryptoWall, check out <a href="https://www.cryptowalltracker.org/" target="_blank" title="CryptoWall Tracker">CryptoWall Tracker</a>)</li>
<li>TorrentLocker</li>
<li>PadCrypt</li>
<li>Locky</li>
<li>CTB-Locker</li>
<li>FAKBEN</li>
<li>PayCrypt</li></ul>
<p>New submissions for Ransomware Tracker are warmly welcome. You can send new additions to <strong>rt-RintANel@abuse.ch</strong> (remove all letters in uppercase). Malware binaries that you suspect to be associated with a certain Ransomware family can be send to <strong>rt-malwSOareM@abuse.ch</strong> (remove all letters in uppercase) for analysis.</p>
<p>Below is a list of Ransomware botnet C&amp;C servers tracked by Ransomware Tracker. You have the possibility to filter the list below using certain pre-defined filters shown below.</p>
